# UWorld-Anki Note-Level Local Source Map

This map is formatted for fast searching in GitHub or the browser. Search for a term from an Anki note, then use the `UWorld refs` and `Search anchors` fields to find the matching local UWorld question or passage. Explicit UWorld QIDs were not visible in the available sources, so references use local source file names plus question/passage numbers and short source-search anchors.

## Search Tips

- Search flashcard wording with `Flashcard:` plus a distinctive term, eg `Flashcard: lactate`.
- Search source files with the exact phrase listed under `Search anchors`.
- Each entry is note/concept-level, so redundant Anki cards may be collapsed into the clearest searchable note.

## AminoAcids - Classifications.txt

### AminoAcids-Classifications-0001

**Flashcard:** Amino acids that can act as nucleophiles... 1. Serine (Ser/S) 2. Threonine (Thr/T) 3. Tyrosine (Tyr/Y) 4. Cysteine (Cys/C) 5. Lysine (Lys/K)

**UWorld refs:** 01-All-Uworld-Files.pdf / Question 5 of 6; 01-All-Uworld-Files.pdf / Question 3 of 10

**Search anchors:** "act serine threonine"; "act serine cysteine"

### Biochemistry-Membranes-0004

**Flashcard:** Scramblase catalyzes the simultaneous transverse diffusion of two phospholipids in the bilayer - ATP is not required.

**Search anchors:** "simultaneous bilayer atp"
